
'[QUESTION:
Do we have guilds right away, or parties to start?

Alchemy Lab (alchemist mask)
Tailor (tailor mask) -> Let's the player customize their costume
Pet Trainer (Pet Trainer mask)
Cemetery (Grim Reaper mask)
Mine (Miner mask)
Curio (Curiosity Shop mask)
Fortune Teller (Fortune mask) -> Gives the player tips and hints about special events, etc
Town Guide (Guide mask) -> Leads the player through the beginning of the game and gives them information about how to play the game
Casino -> (Casino mask) The player can "gamble" and win "lotteries" to get certain rewards, etc

*Perhaps special maps are actually guilds in and of themselves, and as such they would also contain the living quarters for the members of that guild, to show how close knit they all are as a group, reinforcing that mindset in the player?

Guild Map
Guild Castle (Guild members can hang out there)

City
Arena (Arena Mask -> players can battle each other in there)

Assassin (Assassin mask)
Teaches player how to be a deadly assassin


Be sure to cover the sounds and music and art assets that will be needed for each map/building on a per building basis

The game is based around guilds, and the masks you can join for it. This can combine to create an overall world based notoriety for guildâ€™s at certain points, as there will eventually likely be one big main overworld that people can join (based on stress testing). Either way, the main mechanic is parties/guilds that you can join that are aligned with the masks you use, etc.

Moveable Houses are furnished with some one of the furniture sets that players can get, accounting for the size of the house, naturally

Note: The player doesnâ€™t just level up, the masks do as well

# Game Design
## Summary
The player is a fledgling Masker who is about to embark on a journey to become the worldâ€™s most renowned Masker. They meet many different Maskers and enemies along the way.
## Mindset
Player is goal oriented, and ambitious. Player can take their time to fulfill their goals, or speed up the achievement of them with in-app purchases. The player is able to play the game at their own pace, and for their own enjoyment, as they define their own goals within the game world they inhabit.
## Platforms
Journey is built for iOS and Android platforms.
## Gameplay
The goal of the game is to collect all the masks available. Obstacles are NPCs, enemies, other Maskers, and other players.
## Lore
Maskless are enemies that are causing bad times for everybody (they have hoods and you canâ€™t see their face as they have no mask)
## Multiplayer
*Player has control of their own village, and other plays can visit it*
*Player can join parties and go on quests/adventures in overworld maps*
*Player can join guild and go on quests/adventures in overworld maps, as well as all guild members get access to a shared guild map that is only for their guild and they can customize it accordingly together in a shared ownership kind of way*
*All players can access and visit a centralized, global city that houses all players, this city would serve as a lobby of sorts.*
*Guilds can invade and attack other guild maps in real time*
## Art
*What kinds of colors will you be using? Do you have a limited palette to work with? A post-processed HSV map/image? Consistency is key for immersion.*

*What kind of graphic style are you going for? Cartoony? Pixel-y? Cute? How, specifically? Solid, thick outlines with flat hues? Non-black outlines with limited tints/shades? Emphasize smooth curvatures over sharp angles? Describe a set of general rules depicting your style here.*

*Well-designed feedback, both good (e.g. leveling up) and bad (e.g. being hit), are great for teaching the player how to play through trial and error, instead of scripting a lengthy tutorial. What kind of visual feedback are you going to use to let the player know theyâ€™re interacting with something? That they **can** interact with something?*
## Music
*Again, consistency is key. Define that consistency here. What kind of instruments do you want to use in your music? Any particular tempo, key? Influences, genre? Mood?*

*Stylistically, what kind of sound effects are you looking for? Do you want to exaggerate actions with lengthy, cartoony sounds (e.g. marioâ€™s jump), or use just enough to let the player know something happened (e.g. mega manâ€™s landing)? Going for realism? You can use the music style as a bit of a reference too.*
    
*Remember, auditory feedback should stand out from the music and other sound effects so the player hears it well. Volume, panning, and frequency/pitch are all important aspects to consider in both music and sounds - so plan accordingly!*
## Currency
The currency in the game is called Notes, and the player can earn them through taking on quests, defeating enemies, and selling their items to vendors or performing for the NPCs in the game. Notes can also be obtained via in-app purchase. *(maybe)*

## Wandering Adventurers
Wandering Adventurers appear at specific times within the playerâ€™s town, and rumors about them showing up can always be heard in the days leading up to the events. Wanderers are special in that they offer the player one-off bonuses or perks during their visit, and then they leave town until adventure brings them back again. A wandering adventurer will stay in the playerâ€™s town for 24 hours upon their arrival.
### Assassin
    - Shows up when: Itâ€™s a full moon and the wind is blowing to the east
    - Arrives at: 2:00 AM
    - Quest Details:
    - Reward:
### Shaman
    - Shows up when: Itâ€™s rained three days in a row
    - Arrives at: 6:00 AM
    - Quest Details:
    - Reward:
### Ronin
    - Shows up when: Itâ€™s the first day of Spring in Japan
    - Arrives at: 12:00 PM
    - Quest Details:
    - Reward: Sakkat mask
### Ghost
    - Shows up when: Itâ€™s Halloween
    - Arrives at: 12:00 AM
    - Quest Details:
    - Reward: Ghost Bandana
### Southern Raider
    - Shows up when: Itâ€™s above 30 degrees
    - Arrives at: 5:00 AM
    - Quest Details:
    - Reward: Southern Raider Mask
### Blue Spirit
    - Shows up when: Itâ€™s fall
    - Arrives at: 12:00 AM
    - Quest Details:
    - Reward: Blue Spirit Mask

# Maps
A compilation of potential maps that could be featured in the game, and their purposes. Overworld parts of the map will be obscured by fog of war to encourage the player to explore and to fill out their Cartography map. The map will also contain ten preset houses that the player can move into.
## Town
### Buildings
### NPCs
### Quests

### Quests

## Overworld
### Buildings

### Quests 



# Items
## Masks
Masks are able to be leveled, and certain masks will be more powerful and more rare than others. Every mask has a second phase of evolution, and potentially a third final phase as well. Digimon Style. The mask that the user is currently wearing also determines the weapon they are equipped with.

## Furniture
Furniture can be used to customize the playerâ€™s house to their liking. It comes in a variety of sets and themes, and there are certain unique pieces that will require the player to either craft on their own, or get from a wandering adventurer or difficult quest.
### Grid Sizes
    - Small (1x1)
    - Medium (1x2)
    - Large (2x2)
### Furniture Series 
    (Each Furniture Series has 25 items in it's set, including matching wallpaper and flooring)

## Day Night Cycle
### Requirements: 
    - Update in-game weather based on userâ€™s current location
    - Weather API integration
    - Return Weather API results as in-game Weather states
### Resources:

## Weather Cycle
### Requirements:
### Resources:

## System time integration
### Requirements:
### Resources: 

## Time Based Events
### Requirements:
    - Mask Creation Time System (player is notified when their mask has finished crafting)
    - Unique NPCs show up based on certain times (i.e. Santa shows up on Christmas, and the player is notified via notifications)
    - Unique events can also happen at certain times that will get players special items
### Resources:

## Chat System
### Requirements:
    - Photon PUN+ chat integration
### Resources:

## NPCs
### Requirements:
    - Dialogue Tree System
    - Time Based Behaviours
    - Wandering Behaviour
### Resources:

## Enemies
### Requirements:
    - Combat System
    - Time Based Appearances
    - Weaknesses to certain masks
### Resources:

##Monetization
### Requirements:
    - In-App Purchases
### Resources:

## House Customization
### Requirements:
    - Grid System
    - Furniture Management

## Inventory
### Requirements:
    - Inventory System
### Resources:

## Status
### Requirements:
    - Character stats and level
### Resources:

## Equipment
### Requirements:
    - Character Equipment
### Resources:

## Character Customization
### Requirements:
    - Character Skins
    - Character Models
    - Character Weapons
### Resources:

## Combat
### Requirements:
    - Dynamic Camera System
    - Gesture and Swipe Detection System
    - Depth based combat
    - Combos and unique attacks based on certain swipes and gestures
### Resources:

## Guilds
### Requirements:
    - Create a guild
    - Join a guild
    - Leave guild
    - Disband guild
    - Centralized guild map
### Resources:

## Parties
### Requirements:
    - Create a party
    - Join a party
    - Leave party
    - Disband party

## Masks
### Requirements:
    - Mask level up system
    - Certain masks transform the character into different beings
### Resources:

## Cutscenes
### Requirements:
    - Beginning cutscene to welcome and onboard the player to the game and gather the following information
    - Name
    - Gender
    - Character Customization Options
    - Access to Location (for real time weather and day night cycle)
    - Access to Notifications (for notifying player of upcoming events)
### Resources:

## Crafting
### Requirements:
    - Ability to make masks via ingredients found throughout the world
    - Ability to combine masks from other masks/ingredients to make new, specialized powerful masks
### Resources:

## Quests
### Requirements:
    - Ability to go on quests
    - Quests log
### Resources:

## Pets
### Requirements:
    - Pets that follow the player around, and potentially do combat.
### Resources:

## Mounts
### Requirements:
    - Ability to ride horses and other animals around the world.
### Resources:

## Relationships
### Requirements:
    - Ability to build up friendships with NPCs, and receive perks in form of discounts, free gifts, etc. from them in return.
### Resources:







# Development
## Technology Stack
    - Game Engine: Unity
    - Texture Creation: Photoshop
    - 3D Model Creation: Blender
    - Animation:
    - Programming: Sublime Text
    - Documentation: Github
    - Multiplayer: Photon PUN+
    - Chat: Photon Chat
    - Server Backend: Parse
    - Game Analytics:
    - In-App Purchases: Parse
    - Notifications: Parse
    - Bug Tracking:

## Derived Components / Component Compositions
